# Scripts cmd

This file show the scripts command used for my PhD dissertation.

## Reservoir

Use GAGES dataset to train.

### normal models

Because we have trained models in this paper: https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jhydrol.2021.126455 , We only run script to
generate config file and directly evaluate model.

```Shell
# LSTM for CAMELS 523: 6 random seeds -- 1234, 123, 12345, 111, 1111, 11111
python train_evaluate.py --sub gages/exp311 --source GAGES --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/gages --download 0 --model_name KuaiLSTM --model_param {\"n_input_features\":37\,\"n_output_features\":1\,\"n_hidden_states\":256} --weight_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/exp311/model_Ep300.pth --continue_train 0 --opt Adadelta --loss_func RMSESum --rs 1234 --cache_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/exp311 --cache_read 1 --train_period 1990-01-01 2000-01-01 --test_period 2000-01-01 2010-01-01 --scaler DapengScaler --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --train_epoch 300 --te 300 --save_epoch 50 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_c DRAIN_SQKM ELEV_MEAN_M_BASIN SLOPE_PCT DEVNLCD06 FORESTNLCD06 PLANTNLCD06 WATERNLCD06 SNOWICENLCD06 BARRENNLCD06 SHRUBNLCD06 GRASSNLCD06 WOODYWETNLCD06 EMERGWETNLCD06 AWCAVE PERMAVE RFACT ROCKDEPAVE GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM_PCT STREAMS_KM_SQ_KM NDAMS_2009 STOR_NOR_2009 RAW_DIS_NEAREST_MAJ_DAM CANALS_PCT RAW_DIS_NEAREST_CANAL FRESHW_WITHDRAWAL POWER_SUM_MW PDEN_2000_BLOCK ROADS_KM_SQ_KM IMPNLCD06 --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/gages523.csv
# LSTM for CONUS 3557: 6 random seeds -- 1234, 123, 12345, 111, 1111, 11111
python train_evaluate.py --sub gages/exp317 --source GAGES --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/gages --download 0 --model_name KuaiLSTM --model_param {\"n_input_features\":37\,\"n_output_features\":1\,\"n_hidden_states\":256} --weight_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/exp317/model_Ep300.pth --continue_train 0 --opt Adadelta --loss_func RMSESum --rs 1234 --cache_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/exp317 --cache_read 1 --train_period 1990-01-01 2000-01-01 --test_period 2000-01-01 2010-01-01 --scaler DapengScaler --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --train_epoch 300 --te 300 --save_epoch 50 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_c DRAIN_SQKM ELEV_MEAN_M_BASIN SLOPE_PCT DEVNLCD06 FORESTNLCD06 PLANTNLCD06 WATERNLCD06 SNOWICENLCD06 BARRENNLCD06 SHRUBNLCD06 GRASSNLCD06 WOODYWETNLCD06 EMERGWETNLCD06 AWCAVE PERMAVE RFACT ROCKDEPAVE GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM_PCT STREAMS_KM_SQ_KM NDAMS_2009 STOR_NOR_2009 RAW_DIS_NEAREST_MAJ_DAM CANALS_PCT RAW_DIS_NEAREST_CANAL FRESHW_WITHDRAWAL POWER_SUM_MW PDEN_2000_BLOCK ROADS_KM_SQ_KM IMPNLCD06 --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/3557basins_ID_NSE_DOR.csv
# LSTM for pair1 zero-dor + small-dor: 6 random seeds -- 1234, 123, 12345, 111, 1111, 11111
python train_evaluate.py --sub gages/exp331 --source GAGES --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/gages --download 0 --model_name KuaiLSTM --model_param {\"n_input_features\":37\,\"n_output_features\":1\,\"n_hidden_states\":256} --weight_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/exp331/model_Ep300.pth --continue_train 0 --opt Adadelta --loss_func RMSESum --rs 1234 --cache_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/exp331 --cache_read 1 --train_period 1990-01-01 2000-01-01 --test_period 2000-01-01 2010-01-01 --scaler DapengScaler --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --train_epoch 300 --te 300 --save_epoch 50 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_c DRAIN_SQKM ELEV_MEAN_M_BASIN SLOPE_PCT DEVNLCD06 FORESTNLCD06 PLANTNLCD06 WATERNLCD06 SNOWICENLCD06 BARRENNLCD06 SHRUBNLCD06 GRASSNLCD06 WOODYWETNLCD06 EMERGWETNLCD06 AWCAVE PERMAVE RFACT ROCKDEPAVE GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM_PCT STREAMS_KM_SQ_KM NDAMS_2009 STOR_NOR_2009 RAW_DIS_NEAREST_MAJ_DAM CANALS_PCT RAW_DIS_NEAREST_CANAL FRESHW_WITHDRAWAL POWER_SUM_MW PDEN_2000_BLOCK ROADS_KM_SQ_KM IMPNLCD06 --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/3557basins_ID_NSE_DOR.csv
```

### pub models

```Shell
# LSTM for PUBs
# pub-zs: train train-z-zs
python train_evaluate.py --sub gages/exp34001 --source GAGES --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/gages --download 0 --model_name KuaiLSTM --model_param {\"n_input_features\":37\,\"n_output_features\":1\,\"n_hidden_states\":256} --opt Adadelta --loss_func RMSESum --rs 1234 --cache_write 1 --cache_read 1 --train_period 1990-01-01 2000-01-01 --test_period 2000-01-01 2010-01-01 --scaler DapengScaler --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --train_epoch 300 --te 300 --save_epoch 20 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_c DRAIN_SQKM ELEV_MEAN_M_BASIN SLOPE_PCT DEVNLCD06 FORESTNLCD06 PLANTNLCD06 WATERNLCD06 SNOWICENLCD06 BARRENNLCD06 SHRUBNLCD06 GRASSNLCD06 WOODYWETNLCD06 EMERGWETNLCD06 AWCAVE PERMAVE RFACT ROCKDEPAVE GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM_PCT STREAMS_KM_SQ_KM NDAMS_2009 STOR_NOR_2009 RAW_DIS_NEAREST_MAJ_DAM CANALS_PCT RAW_DIS_NEAREST_CANAL FRESHW_WITHDRAWAL POWER_SUM_MW PDEN_2000_BLOCK ROADS_KM_SQ_KM IMPNLCD06 --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/gages_train_z_zs0.csv
python train_evaluate.py --sub gages/exp34002 --source GAGES --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/gages --download 0 --ctx 1 --model_name KuaiLSTM --model_param {\"n_input_features\":37\,\"n_output_features\":1\,\"n_hidden_states\":256} --opt Adadelta --loss_func RMSESum --rs 1234 --cache_write 1 --cache_read 1 --train_period 1990-01-01 2000-01-01 --test_period 2000-01-01 2010-01-01 --scaler DapengScaler --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --train_epoch 300 --te 300 --save_epoch 20 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_c DRAIN_SQKM ELEV_MEAN_M_BASIN SLOPE_PCT DEVNLCD06 FORESTNLCD06 PLANTNLCD06 WATERNLCD06 SNOWICENLCD06 BARRENNLCD06 SHRUBNLCD06 GRASSNLCD06 WOODYWETNLCD06 EMERGWETNLCD06 AWCAVE PERMAVE RFACT ROCKDEPAVE GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM_PCT STREAMS_KM_SQ_KM NDAMS_2009 STOR_NOR_2009 RAW_DIS_NEAREST_MAJ_DAM CANALS_PCT RAW_DIS_NEAREST_CANAL FRESHW_WITHDRAWAL POWER_SUM_MW PDEN_2000_BLOCK ROADS_KM_SQ_KM IMPNLCD06 --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/gages_train_z_zs1.csv
# pub-zl: train train-z-zl
python train_evaluate.py --sub gages/exp34003 --source GAGES --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/gages --download 0 --model_name KuaiLSTM --model_param {\"n_input_features\":37\,\"n_output_features\":1\,\"n_hidden_states\":256} --opt Adadelta --loss_func RMSESum --rs 1234 --cache_write 1 --cache_read 1 --train_period 1990-01-01 2000-01-01 --test_period 2000-01-01 2010-01-01 --scaler DapengScaler --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --train_epoch 300 --te 300 --save_epoch 20 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_c DRAIN_SQKM ELEV_MEAN_M_BASIN SLOPE_PCT DEVNLCD06 FORESTNLCD06 PLANTNLCD06 WATERNLCD06 SNOWICENLCD06 BARRENNLCD06 SHRUBNLCD06 GRASSNLCD06 WOODYWETNLCD06 EMERGWETNLCD06 AWCAVE PERMAVE RFACT ROCKDEPAVE GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM_PCT STREAMS_KM_SQ_KM NDAMS_2009 STOR_NOR_2009 RAW_DIS_NEAREST_MAJ_DAM CANALS_PCT RAW_DIS_NEAREST_CANAL FRESHW_WITHDRAWAL POWER_SUM_MW PDEN_2000_BLOCK ROADS_KM_SQ_KM IMPNLCD06 --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/gages_train_z_zl0.csv
python train_evaluate.py --sub gages/exp34004 --source GAGES --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/gages --download 0 --ctx 1 --model_name KuaiLSTM --model_param {\"n_input_features\":37\,\"n_output_features\":1\,\"n_hidden_states\":256} --opt Adadelta --loss_func RMSESum --rs 1234 --cache_write 1 --cache_read 1 --train_period 1990-01-01 2000-01-01 --test_period 2000-01-01 2010-01-01 --scaler DapengScaler --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --train_epoch 300 --te 300 --save_epoch 20 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_c DRAIN_SQKM ELEV_MEAN_M_BASIN SLOPE_PCT DEVNLCD06 FORESTNLCD06 PLANTNLCD06 WATERNLCD06 SNOWICENLCD06 BARRENNLCD06 SHRUBNLCD06 GRASSNLCD06 WOODYWETNLCD06 EMERGWETNLCD06 AWCAVE PERMAVE RFACT ROCKDEPAVE GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM GEOL_REEDBUSH_DOM_PCT STREAMS_KM_SQ_KM NDAMS_2009 STOR_NOR_2009 RAW_DIS_NEAREST_MAJ_DAM CANALS_PCT RAW_DIS_NEAREST_CANAL FRESHW_WITHDRAWAL POWER_SUM_MW PDEN_2000_BLOCK ROADS_KM_SQ_KM IMPNLCD06 --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/gages/gages_train_z_zl1.csv
```

## Multi-output model

### Single-task

```Shell
python train_evaluate.py --sub camels/exp41501 --source CAMELS_FLOW_ET --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/camelsflowet /mnt/data/owen411/data/modiset4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/camels/camels_us /mnt/data/owen411/data/nldas4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/smap4camels --download 0 --ctx 0 --model_name KuaiLSTMMultiOut --model_param {\"n_input_features\":23\,\"n_output_features\":2\,\"n_hidden_states\":256\,\"layer_hidden_size\":128} --loss_func MultiOutLoss --loss_param {\"loss_funcs\":\"RMSESum\"\,\"data_gap\":[0\,2]\,\"device\":[0]\,\"item_weight\":[1.0\,0.0]\,\"limit_part\":[1]} --cache_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/exp41013 --cache_read 1 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_t total_precipitation potential_evaporation temperature specific_humidity shortwave_radiation potential_energy --var_t_type nldas --var_out usgsFlow ET --train_period 2001-10-01 2011-10-01 --test_period 2011-10-01 2016-10-01 --opt Adadelta --rs 1234 --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --scaler DapengScaler --n_output 2 --train_epoch 300 --save_epoch 20 --te 300 --fill_nan no mean --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/camels_us_mtl_2001_2021_flow_screen.csv
python train_evaluate.py --sub camels/exp41502 --source CAMELS_FLOW_ET --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/camelsflowet /mnt/data/owen411/data/modiset4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/camels/camels_us /mnt/data/owen411/data/nldas4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/smap4camels --download 0 --ctx 1 --model_name KuaiLSTMMultiOut --model_param {\"n_input_features\":23\,\"n_output_features\":2\,\"n_hidden_states\":256\,\"layer_hidden_size\":128} --loss_func MultiOutLoss --loss_param {\"loss_funcs\":\"RMSESum\"\,\"data_gap\":[0\,2]\,\"device\":[1]\,\"item_weight\":[0.0\,1.0]\,\"limit_part\":[0]} --cache_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/exp41013 --cache_read 1 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_t total_precipitation potential_evaporation temperature specific_humidity shortwave_radiation potential_energy --var_t_type nldas --var_out usgsFlow ET --train_period 2001-10-01 2011-10-01 --test_period 2011-10-01 2016-10-01 --opt Adadelta --rs 1234 --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --scaler DapengScaler --n_output 2 --train_epoch 300 --save_epoch 20 --te 300 --fill_nan no mean --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/camels_us_mtl_2001_2021_flow_screen.csv
```

### Variable Prediction Improvement

```Shell
# ET -> flow Multi-Layers; flow:et = 1:1
python train_evaluate.py --sub camels/exp41301 --source CAMELS_FLOW_ET --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/camelsflowet /mnt/data/owen411/data/modiset4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/camels/camels_us /mnt/data/owen411/data/nldas4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/smap4camels --download 0 --ctx 0 --model_name KuaiLSTMMultiOut --model_param {\"n_input_features\":23\,\"n_output_features\":2\,\"n_hidden_states\":256\,\"layer_hidden_size\":128} --loss_func MultiOutLoss --loss_param {\"loss_funcs\":\"RMSESum\"\,\"data_gap\":[0\,2]\,\"device\":[0]\,\"item_weight\":[0.5\,0.5]} --cache_write 1 --cache_read 1 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_t total_precipitation potential_evaporation temperature specific_humidity shortwave_radiation potential_energy --var_t_type nldas --var_out usgsFlow ET --train_period 2001-10-01 2006-10-01 --test_period 2006-10-01 2011-10-01 --opt Adadelta --rs 1234 --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --scaler DapengScaler --n_output 2 --train_epoch 300 --save_epoch 20 --te 300 --fill_nan no mean --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/camels_us_mtl_2001_2021_flow_screen.csv
# ET -> flow Multi-Layers; flow:et = 3:1
python train_evaluate.py --sub camels/exp41307 --source CAMELS_FLOW_ET --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/camelsflowet /mnt/data/owen411/data/modiset4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/camels/camels_us /mnt/data/owen411/data/nldas4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/smap4camels --download 0 --ctx 1 --model_name KuaiLSTMMultiOut --model_param {\"n_input_features\":23\,\"n_output_features\":2\,\"n_hidden_states\":256\,\"layer_hidden_size\":128} --loss_func MultiOutLoss --loss_param {\"loss_funcs\":\"RMSESum\"\,\"data_gap\":[0\,2]\,\"device\":[1]\,\"item_weight\":[0.75\,0.25]} --cache_read 1 --cache_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/exp41301 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_t total_precipitation potential_evaporation temperature specific_humidity shortwave_radiation potential_energy --var_t_type nldas --var_out usgsFlow ET --train_period 2001-10-01 2006-10-01 --test_period 2006-10-01 2011-10-01 --opt Adadelta --rs 1234 --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --scaler DapengScaler --n_output 2 --train_epoch 300 --save_epoch 20 --te 300 --fill_nan no mean --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/camels_us_mtl_2001_2021_flow_screen.csv

# ET -> flow Multi-Layers; flow:et = 24:1
python train_evaluate.py --sub camels/exp41319 --source CAMELS_FLOW_ET --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/camelsflowet /mnt/data/owen411/data/modiset4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/camels/camels_us /mnt/data/owen411/data/nldas4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/smap4camels --download 0 --ctx 1 --model_name KuaiLSTMMultiOut --model_param {\"n_input_features\":23\,\"n_output_features\":2\,\"n_hidden_states\":256\,\"layer_hidden_size\":128} --loss_func MultiOutLoss --loss_param {\"loss_funcs\":\"RMSESum\"\,\"data_gap\":[0\,2]\,\"device\":[1]\,\"item_weight\":[0.96\,0.04]} --cache_read 1 --cache_path /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/exp41301 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_t total_precipitation potential_evaporation temperature specific_humidity shortwave_radiation potential_energy --var_t_type nldas --var_out usgsFlow ET --train_period 2001-10-01 2006-10-01 --test_period 2006-10-01 2011-10-01 --opt Adadelta --rs 1234 --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --scaler DapengScaler --n_output 2 --train_epoch 300 --save_epoch 20 --te 300 --fill_nan no mean --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/camels_us_mtl_2001_2021_flow_screen.csv
```

```Shell
python train_evaluate.py --sub camels/exp436 --download 0 --ctx 1 --source NLDAS_CAMELS --source_path /mnt/data/owen411/data/nldas4camels /mnt/data/owen411/data/camels/camels_us --source_region US --model_name KuaiLSTM --model_param {\"n_input_features\":23\,\"n_output_features\":1\,\"n_hidden_states\":256} --opt Adadelta --loss_func RMSESum --rs 1234 --cache_read 1 --cache_write 1 --train_period 2015-04-01 2019-10-01 --test_period 2020-10-01 2021-10-01 --scaler DapengScaler --data_loader StreamflowDataModel --train_epoch 300 --save_epoch 50 --te 300 --batch_size 100 --rho 365 --var_t total_precipitation potential_evaporation temperature specific_humidity shortwave_radiation potential_energy --gage_id_file /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/exp43_kfold6/camels_train_kfold5.csv

python /mnt/data/owen411/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/app/screen_cmds.py -S exp437 exp438 exp439 exp4310 exp4311 exp4312 -C 0 1 0 1 0 1 -W 0.5 0.5 -W 0.5 0.5 -W 0.5 0.5 -W 0.5 0.5 -W 0.5 0.5 -W 0.5 0.5 -K 0 1 2 3 4 5
```

## dPL models

This part is run in a Windows server computer.

### CAMELS-CC

First exp for dPL is for basins in Three Gorges.

```Shell
# dPL xaj attr single-layer ann for CAMELS-CC
python train_evaluate.py --sub camels/exp511 --source CAMELS --source_path E:/owen/data/camels/camels_cc --source_region CC --ctx -1 --download 0 --model_name DplAttrXaj --opt Adadelta --rs 1234 --cache_write 1 --cache_read 1 --model_param {\"n_input_features\":25,\"n_output_features\":15,\"n_hidden_states\":256,\"dr\":0.2,\"warmup_length\":365,\"kernel_size\":15,\"param_limit_func\":\"clamp\"} --scaler DapengScaler --scaler_params {\"basin_norm_cols\":[\"Q\"],\"gamma_norm_cols\":[\"total_precipitation\",\"potential_evaporation\"]} --warmup_length 365 --data_loader DplDataModel --loss_func RMSESum --batch_size 10 --rho 365 --train_epoch 100 --te 100 --save_epoch 10 --var_t total_precipitation potential_evaporation temperature_2m dewpoint_temperature_2m surface_net_solar_radiation snow_depth_water_equivalent --var_c p_mean pet_mean aet_mean aridity p_seasonality high_prec_freq high_prec_dur high_prec_timing low_prec_freq low_prec_dur low_prec_timing frac_snow_daily geol_class_1st geol_class_1st_frac MixedForest permeability porosity root_depth_50 root_depth_99 BDTICM_M_250m_ll SNDPPT CLYPPT elev slope Area --var_out Q --target_as_input 0 --constant_only 1 --train_period 2014-10-01 2020-10-01 --test_period 2019-10-01 2021-10-01 --gage_id_file E:/owen/code/HydroSPB/hydroSPB/example/camels/camels_cc_2014_2020_flow_screen.csv
```

### CAMELS-US

Use CAMELS dataset to train dPL models

As there are many loops and un-optimized code for GPU, the speed in CPU is faster.


## Transfer learning

### Reservoir streamflow Transfer Learning
